	UKR_hetman_makes_his_move = {
		icon = GFX_decision_shield
		
		allowed = { always = no } #manually activated
		
		cancel_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = UKR_Prepare_The_Anti_Hetman_Coup
		}
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = UKR_Prepare_The_Anti_Hetman_Coup
		}
		
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 35
		
		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_hetman_makes_his_move"
			UKR_decrease_hetman_strength = yes
			UKR_decrease_hetman = yes
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout UKR_hetman_makes_his_move"
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = UKR_Coalition_With_UVO }
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_1 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_1
					country_event = ukrpol.301
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_2 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_2
					country_event = ukrpol.17
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_3 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_3
					country_event = ukrpol.27
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_4 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_4
					country_event = ukrpol.28
				}
				else = {
					UKR_increase_hetman_strength = yes
					UKR_increase_hetman = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = UKR_Coalition_Of_Monarchists }
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_1 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_1
					country_event = ukrpol.29
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_2 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_2
					country_event = ukrpol.30
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_3 }
					}
					set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move_3
					country_event = ukrpol.19
					hidden_effect = {
						country_event = {
							id = ukrpol.20
							days = 15
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					UKR_increase_hetman_strength = yes
					UKR_increase_hetman = yes
				}
			}
			activate_mission = UKR_hetman_makes_his_move
		}

				}
			}
			OR = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = UKR_rivne_uprising_trigger
					check_variable = { UKR_Direktoriia_Strength_real < 0.25 }

			}
		}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = "The regime has stabilized"

					has_global_flag = UKR_dnieper_explosion
					has_global_flag = UKR_hetmanate_is_over
					has_global_flag = UKR_konovalets_counet_coup
				}
			}			
			OR = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = UKR_rivne_uprising_trigger
					check_variable = { UKR_Direktoriia_Strength_real < 0.25 }
				}
				country_exists = WSU
				has_global_flag = UPR_dyrektoria_joined_peacefully
			}
		}
		
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 220
		
		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_rivne_uprising"
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_global_flag = UPR_dyrektoria_joined_peacefully }
				}
				country_event = ukrpol.37
				set_global_flag = UPR_dyrektoria_become_exiled_in_WSU
			}
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout UKR_rivne_uprising"
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_RIVNE_UPRISING option = UKR_RIVNE_UPRISING_DYREKTORIA_DISABLED }
				}
				country_event = ukrpol.37
				set_global_flag = UPR_dyrektoria_become_exiled_in_WSU
			}
			else = {
				country_event = ukrpol.36
			}
		}
	}

political_actions = {
	UKR_recruit_teroborona = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military

		allowed = { tag = UKR }
		
		available = {
			has_war_support > 0			
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = UKR_teroborona_is_recruiting
			}
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = { FROM = { has_state_flag = UKR_teroborona_recruited_@ROOT } }
			has_defensive_war = yes
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 499 }
			command_power > 4
		}
		custom_cost_text = 500_infantry_equipment_1_cp_5
		days_remove = 15
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		on_map_mode = map_only

		state_target = yes
		target_array = UKR.owned_states
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		target_root_trigger = {
			has_idea = UKR_teroborona_idea
			has_defensive_war = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision cancel UKR_recruit_teroborona target: [From.GetName]"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = 5
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 500
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_recruit_teroborona target: [From.GetName]"
			set_country_flag = UKR_teroborona_is_recruiting
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -5
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -500
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove UKR_recruit_teroborona target: [From.GetName]"
			clr_country_flag = UKR_teroborona_is_recruiting
			FROM = {
				set_state_flag = UKR_teroborona_recruited_@ROOT
				### calculate number of units to spawn
				set_temp_variable = { units_to_spawn = state_population_k }
				divide_temp_variable = { units_to_spawn = 500 }

				### failsafe so at least one unit is always spawned
				clamp_temp_variable = { var = units_to_spawn min = 1 max = 7 }

				### tooltip
				set_temp_variable = { total_units_to_spawn = units_to_spawn }
				custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_recruit_teroborona_units

				### spawn normal militias
				set_temp_variable = { counter = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { var = units_to_spawn value = 1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
					}
					ROOT = { 
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_template = "Teroborona" }
							}
							division_template = {
								name = "Teroborona"
								division_names_group = UKR_MIL_01
								regiments = {
									militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
									militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
									militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
									militia = { x = 2 y = 0 }
									militia = { x = 2 y = 1 }
									militia = { x = 2 y = 2 }
								}
								support = {
									recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
									military_police = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								}
								priority = 0
							}
						}
					}
					for_loop_effect = {
						start = 1
						end = units_to_spawn
						compare = less_than_or_equals

						meta_effect = {
							text = {
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = [DIVISION] division_template = \"Teroborona\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 1"
									allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
									owner = ROOT
								}
							}
							DIVISION = "\\\"[?counter]a [THIS.GetName] Okrema Bryhada Teritorialnoi Oborony\\\""
						}
						add_to_temp_variable = { counter = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		icon = generic_agreement
		name = UKR_Join_Revolutionary_Fray

		available = {
			at_peace_or_same_enemies_as_FROM = yes			
		}

		visible = {
			is_subject = no

			UKR_richytskyi_in_power = no

				has_socialist_government = yes
				is_faction_leader = no
			}

UKR_foreign_policy = {
	UKR_evacuate_industry = {
		allowed = { is_ukrainian_tag = yes }
		priority = 10
		icon = generic_construction
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				surrender_progress < 0.01
			}
		}
		state_target = yes

		targets = { 221 227 228 200 1239 1283 1282 1284 1285 1286 }

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_core_of = ROOT
				is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
				OR = { #Has at least 2 factories
					arms_factory > 1
					industrial_complex > 1
					AND = {
						arms_factory > 0
						industrial_complex > 0
					}
				}
				infrastructure > 1
			}
		}
		target_root_trigger = {
			has_civil_war = no
			has_war_with = var:219.owner
		}

		available = {
			FROM = {
				is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
				infrastructure > 2
			}
			has_equipment = { train_equipment > 39 } #10 trains per factory
		}		
		cancel_if_not_visible = no
		cost = 25
		days_remove = 30
		complete_effect = {  #Attempt to remove 2 CIVS & 2 MILS
			hidden_effect = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = train_equipment
					amount = -40
					producer = UKR
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_industry_relocation_trains_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_industry_relocation_complete_effect_tt
			#REMOVE factories
			FROM = {
				hidden_effect = {
					set_temp_variable = { UKR_factories_counter = 0 }

					#Attempt to relocate 50%-50% of mils-civs
					set_temp_variable = { UKR_half_the_factories_to_relocate = 4 }
					divide_temp_variable = { UKR_half_the_factories_to_relocate = 2 }
					while_loop_effect = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { UKR_factories_counter = 4 compare = less_than }
						}
						if = { #GO MILS (if possible)
							limit = {
								check_variable = { UKR_factories_counter = UKR_half_the_factories_to_relocate compare = less_than }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { arms_factory > 0 }
								remove_building = {
									type = arms_factory
									level = 1
								}
								if = {
									limit = { has_state_flag = UKR_mils_removed_flag }
									modify_state_flag = { flag = UKR_mils_removed_flag value = 1 }
								}
								else = {
									set_state_flag = UKR_mils_removed_flag
								}
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = { industrial_complex > 0 }
								remove_building = {
									type = industrial_complex
									level = 1
								}
								if = {
									limit = { has_state_flag = UKR_civs_removed_flag }
									modify_state_flag = { flag = UKR_civs_removed_flag value = 1 }
								}
								else = {
									set_state_flag = UKR_civs_removed_flag
								}
							}
						}
						else = { #GO CIVS (if possible)
							if = {
								limit = { industrial_complex > 0 }
								remove_building = {
									type = industrial_complex
									level = 1
								}
								if = {
									limit = { has_state_flag = UKR_civs_removed_flag }
									modify_state_flag = { flag = UKR_civs_removed_flag value = 1 }
								}
								else = {
									set_state_flag = UKR_civs_removed_flag
								}
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = { arms_factory > 0 }
								remove_building = {
									type = arms_factory
									level = 1
								}
								if = {
									limit = { has_state_flag = UKR_mils_removed_flag }
									modify_state_flag = { flag = UKR_mils_removed_flag value = 1 }
								}
								else = {
									set_state_flag = UKR_mils_removed_flag
								}
							}
						}
						add_to_temp_variable = { UKR_factories_counter = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = train_equipment
					amount = 40
					producer = UKR
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_industry_relocation_remove_effect_tt
			#RELOCATE FACTORIES
			FROM = {
				set_temp_variable = { UKR_factories_counter = 0 }
				#Factories attempt to get relocated in 2 different states
				set_temp_variable = { UKR_half_the_factories_to_relocate = 4 }
				divide_temp_variable = { UKR_half_the_factories_to_relocate = 2 }
				while_loop_effect = { #NOTE: Due to the seed not changing during the execution of this effect, the same state will always be chosen, UNLESS it runs out of slots -> That's the reason for this
					limit = {
						check_variable = { UKR_factories_counter = UKR_half_the_factories_to_relocate compare = less_than }
					}
					UKR_relocate_industry_in_appropriate_state_effect = yes
					add_to_temp_variable = { UKR_factories_counter = 1 }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_relocate_industry_repair_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_relocate_industry_lose_control_tt
		}
	}

				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote
		}

		targets = { CHI GXC YUN }
		target_root_trigger = { 
			has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote
			has_completed_focus = UKR_Help_Indochina_LKMT
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				any_enemy_country = {
					OR = {
						is_ally_of_major = yes
						is_actual_major = yes
						tag = MAF
						tag = QIE
						tag = FNG
						has_no_african_interests = no
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_socialist_government = yes
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > 24.99
			has_political_power > 9.99
		}
		custom_cost_text = PP_10_CP_25
		
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		days_remove = 14
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				has_political_power < 50
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision cancel KCN_help_lkmt target: [From.GetName]"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = 25
				add_political_power = 10
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KCN_help_lkmt target: [From.GetName]"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -25
				add_political_power = -10
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove KCN_help_lkmt target: [From.GetName]"
			FROM = { country_event = ukrsoc.82 }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = kcn_council_vote }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = FROM decision = KCN_help_lkmt_aid }
			}
		}
	}

	KCN_vote_timer = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_discourse
		allowed = { always = no } #manually activated
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 30
		is_good = no

		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout KCN_vote_timer"
			clr_global_flag = KCN_vote_ongoing
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = KCN_cultural_research_cooperation_vote }
				clr_global_flag = KCN_cultural_research_cooperation_vote
				UKR = { country_event = ukrsoc.72 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = KCN_economic_cooperation_vote }
				clr_global_flag = KCN_economic_cooperation_vote
				UKR = { country_event = ukrsoc.69 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = KCN_candidate_membership_vote }
				clr_global_flag = KCN_candidate_membership_vote
				UKR = { country_event = ukrsoc.79 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = KCN_candidate_membership_revoke }
				clr_global_flag = KCN_candidate_membership_revoke
				UKR = { country_event = ukrsoc.87 }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { global.kcn_yes_votes > global.kcn_no_votes }
					}
					country_event = { id = ukrsoc.68 hours = 2 }
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { id = ukrsoc.67 hours = 2 }
				}
			}
			clear_variable = global.kcn_yes_votes
			clear_variable = global.kcn_no_votes
			clear_variable = global.kcn_abstain_votes
		}
	}

	### PSC Votes ###

	PSC_vote_yes = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_discourse
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = GER
				original_tag = AUS
				original_tag = HUN
				original_tag = UKR
				original_tag = WHR
				original_tag = POL
				original_tag = GAL
				original_tag = CZE
				original_tag = SVK
				original_tag = SLO
				original_tag = CRO
				original_tag = SER
				original_tag = BUL
				original_tag = BOS
				original_tag = WSU
				original_tag = CPU
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
			has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
			}
		}
		visible = {
			is_in_array = {
				array = global.PSC_voters
				value = THIS
			}
		}
		cost = 0
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = { #####
				factor = 0
				tag = GER
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_independent

UKR_Corn_Decisions = {
	UKR_merging_corn_ingridients = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_agreement

		allowed = { always = no } #manually activated

		available = {
			always = no
		}

		is_good = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 10

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout UKR_merging_corn_ingridients"
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_tech = popcorn_tech }
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { UKR_first_ingridient = 1 }
							check_variable = { UKR_second_ingridient = 5 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { UKR_first_ingridient = 5 }
							check_variable = { UKR_second_ingridient = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = { set_technology = { popcorn_tech = 1 popup = yes } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = popcorn_tech_effect	
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_tech = allweathercorn_tech }
					OR = {
						AND = {

	KR_iea_economic_investment = {
		icon = generic_industry
		priority = 40
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = CAN_iedc_invest_year_FROM
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = KR_iea_investment }
						has_country_flag = { flag = KR_iea_investment days > 364 }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = KR_iea_can_invest_FROM
				set_temp_variable = { global.temp = FROM.iea_civ_factories }
				add_to_temp_variable = { global.temp = FROM.iea_mil_factories }
				add_to_temp_variable = { global.temp = FROM.iea_nav_factories }
				multiply_temp_variable = { global.temp = 10 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { global.temp = FROM.num_of_factories }
				check_variable = { var = global.temp value = 0 compare = less_than_or_equals }
			}
		}
		visible = {
			tag = MIZ
			FROM = {
				is_in_array = { global.mizhmoria_economic_tags_array = THIS }
			}
		}
		
		cost = 0
		custom_cost_text = KR_iea_100pp
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = global.mizhmoria_pp_pool
				value = 100
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = no

		target_root_trigger = {
			tag = MIZ
		}

		target_array = global.mizhmoria_economic_tags_array

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = { tag = MIZ }
				is_in_faction_with = MIZ
				is_in_array = { global.mizhmoria_economic_tags_array = THIS }
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision KR_iea_economic_investment target: [From.GetName]"
			subtract_from_variable = { global.mizhmoria_pp_pool = 100 }
			FROM = { country_event = mizhmoria.53 }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				FROM = { num_of_factories > 10 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { FROM.mizhmoria_pp_pool < 25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { FROM.mizhmoria_pp_pool < 50 }
			}
		}
	}

	UKR_rise_an_uprising = {
		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			can_declare_war_on = FROM
		}
		visible = {
			FROM = { owns_state = 91 }
			check_variable = { UKR_galicia_readiness > 1 }
		}

		targets = { 91.OWNER }
		target_root_trigger = { has_country_flag = UKR_preparing_for_galicia_attack }
		target_trigger = {
			can_declare_war_on = FROM
			FROM = { owns_state = 91 }
		}

		cost = 30
		days_remove = 30
		fire_only_once = yes
		war_with_target_on_remove = yes
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					dont_start_major_faction_wars = yes
					ROOT_is_threatened_cautious = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = { # don't do anything if already at war
				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = { #don't attack if...
				factor = 0
				AUS = {
					is_ally_with = FROM 
					is_faction_leader = yes
					has_war = no
				}
				strength_ratio = { tag = AUS ratio > 2.0 } #ROM isn't stronk
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				AUS = { is_ally_with = FROM } #owner of TRS is AUS or AUS-aligned
				strength_ratio = { tag = AUS ratio > 2.0 }
			}
			modifier = { #attack if uprising starts or ROM is stronk (POL version)
				factor = 20
				POL = {
					is_ally_with = FROM
					NOT = { GER = { is_ally_with = PREV } }
				}
				strength_ratio = { tag = POL ratio > 1.0 }
			}
			modifier = { #don't attack if...
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					AUS = { is_ally_with = FROM }
					GER = { is_ally_with = FROM }
				}
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						strength_ratio = { tag = ROOT ratio > 1.0 }
						AND = {
							is_in_faction = yes
							faction_leader = {
								is_faction_leader = yes
								surrender_progress < 0.10
								strength_ratio = { tag = ROOT ratio > 1.0 }
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_subject = yes
							overlord = {
								surrender_progress < 0.10
								strength_ratio = { tag = ROOT ratio > 1.0 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision cancelled UKR_rise_an_uprising target: [From.GetName]"
			clear_decision_attack_AI = yes
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_rise_an_uprising target: [From.GetName]"
			setup_decision_attack_AI = yes
			FROM = { country_event = kr.political.30 } #warning event
			hidden_effect = {
				var:91.owner = {
					save_event_target_as = UKR_galicia_target
				}
				if = {
					limit = { var:91.owner = { tag = GAL } }
					var:91.owner = {
						country_event = {
							id = ukrpol.39
							days = 3
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove UKR_rise_an_uprising target: [From.GetName]"
			clear_decision_attack_AI = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_war_with = event_target:UKR_galicia_target }
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = event_target:UKR_galicia_target
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = UKR_GAL_revolt
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = global.UKR_east_galicia_states
					
					#Remove AUS/HUN/POL armies
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_ally_with = AUS
								is_ally_with = HUN
								is_ally_with = POL
							}
						}
						to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
					}
					
					#Remove resistance
					if = {
						limit = { has_resistance = yes }
						add_resistance = -100
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_galician_collaboration }
					if = {
						limit = { 
							ROOT = { UKR_has_socialist_government = yes }
						}
						ROOT = {
							division_template = {
								name = "Halytska Chervona Hvardiia"
								division_names_group = UKR_MIL_01
								is_locked = yes
								regiments = {
									militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
									militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
									militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
								}
							}
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Halytska Chervona Hvardiia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
							owner = ROOT
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						}
					}
					else = {
						ROOT = {
							division_template = {
								name = "Okrema Halytska Bryhada"
								division_names_group = UKR_MIL_01
								is_locked = yes
								regiments = {
									militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
									militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
									militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
									militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
								}
							}
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Okrema Halytska Bryhada\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
							owner = ROOT
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_government = national_populist }
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_template = "Halytskyi korpus Sichovykh Striltsiv" }
						}
						division_template = {
							name = "Halytskyi korpus Sichovykh Striltsiv"
							division_names_group = UKR_ELI_02
							regiments = {
								elite_infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								elite_infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								elite_infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
								elite_infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
								elite_infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
								elite_infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
								elite_infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
								infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
								infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
							}
							support = {
								artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								engineer = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								recon = { x = 0 y = 2 }
							}
						}
					}
					random_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_in_array = { global.UKR_east_galicia_states = THIS }
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Halytskyi korpus Sichovykh Striltsiv\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
							owner = ROOT
						}
					}
					random_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							is_in_array = { global.UKR_east_galicia_states = THIS }
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Halytskyi korpus Sichovykh Striltsiv\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"

						}

	UKR_impending_failure_mission = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_factory
		
		allowed = { always = no } #manually activated
		
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = UKR_dont_have_impending_failure
					NOT = {
						has_idea = UKR_impending_failure
						has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_1
						has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_2
						has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_3
						has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_4
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_stability > 0.25
					custom_trigger_tooltip = {
						tooltip = UKR_impending_failure_mission_tt
						check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party > 0.5 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = no
		days_mission_timeout = 150
		
		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision cancel UKR_impending_failure_mission"
			add_stability = 0.1
			add_war_support = 0.1
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout UKR_impending_failure_mission"
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_impending_failure }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = UKR_impending_failure
					add_idea = UKR_impending_failure_1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_1 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = UKR_impending_failure_1
					add_idea = UKR_impending_failure_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = UKR_impending_failure_2
					add_idea = UKR_impending_failure_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = UKR_impending_failure_3
					add_idea = UKR_impending_failure_4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_impending_failure_4 }
				add_stability = -0.1
				add_war_support = -0.1
			}
			activate_mission = UKR_impending_failure_mission
		}
	}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove UKR_organize_a_military_parade"
			clr_country_flag = UKR_sun_taken_decision
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_sun_old_guard_10

				limit = { check_variable = { UKR_sun_integralists > 0.05 } }
				add_to_variable = { UKR_sun_integralists = -0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { UKR_sun_nrm = -0.05 }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { UKR_sun_nrm = -0.1 }
			}			
			UKR_clamp_sun_variables = yes			
			add_war_support = 0.03
			increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_3 = yes
			add_to_variable = { UKR_sun_decisions = 1 }
		}
